                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Sounds weirdly specific but ok
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 RULES: 1. NSFW/CW/TW: ENTIRE GROUP. You may see bad things here. You probably will. BE PREPARED. If you find a post too offensive, report it to The Administration and consider blocking the member who posted it. Do not block The Administration. Any further use of warning on posts is at the discretion of the member posting. 2. NO QUESTION POSTS/AMAs/SELFIES HERE. Ask your weirdly specific questions/discourses/poll options to our spinoff group "@Sounds like a weirdly specific question but ok" or some other spinoff group in the “sounds like a weirdly specific… ” universe, or create your own group. 3. BE NICE &amp; NO HATE SPEECH: While generally left-leaning in membership, this is primarily a humor group and has no explicit political affiliations. It will not necessarily be an echo chamber for any particular view (see Rule #3). Keep the politics out of it and the discourse at a minimum whenever possible. Posts, bait, and comments of a political nature will be deleted at the discretion of The Administration. HOWEVER being an blatant sexist, racist, alt-right nazi, MRA, or other such garbage in this group will still get you banned on sight. 4.DON'T BE A JERK: Disagreements are going to occur. Don't be a jerk. Consider walking away when possible. If you feel harassed/bullied or are bothered by someone not following the rules, tag The Administration and block the offending member(s) if need be. Tag the page or the mod team, or report the problematic posts/comments to the mods. 5. You may see good things here. Not every post is intended to be mocked/devalued for it's weirdly-specifiness. If you think your post may cause confusion, add context or be prepared to explain. You may see satire, and that is OK, as long as that satire is weirdly specific. 6. The Administration may delete frequent reposts, obvious bait, posts in explicit violation of Facebook rules, irrelevant stuff that are deemed not weirdly specific enough, or just really really bad. The Administration may decline posts, close commenting on threads (or dumpsterfires), or ban any member who spams, consistently breaks rules and also just because. 6. (invalid) T SHIRT TUESDAY (although we are quite bored of them) Please post your weirdly specific t-shirts, hoodies, and mugs on Tuesdays only. This way we don't get flooded with products, and the folks who enjoy them get a whole day of them! Weirdly specific question/survey/fact/poll/x posts, please go to the question group. 7. This is NOT: a selfie group, a serious support/advice group, a place to air your complaints or stir up drama regarding other groups, Ask Reddit, or a place to discuss your totally normal/boring personal habits. We do not care about your livestream, youtube channel, or music unless it is clearly weirdly specific.

               <div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Movie Set Memes
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Welcome to Movie Set Memes! Your virtual destination for the silly things you see or experience during production whether it be on set, during, or post! Content posted here should be relevant to working behind the scenes in film, tv, and commercials. We have a few rules below to make sure the experience is positive for everyone. 1. No self-promotion. This is not a place to advertise your passion project. 2. NO DOXING (google it). Harassment of any kind will result in a permanent ban. This includes going out of the group and attacking individuals on their personal facebook in reaction to something that gave birth on MSM. 3. No political discussion or trolling politics. Neutral memes with political figures like “Not Bad Obama” is fine if it's relevant but absolutely no arguing politics or using the group to make strong political statements. It never ends well online. 4. No posts/comments that promote sexual assault, sexual harassment, racism, etc. 5. No dissing on actual production companies or crew members because you had a bad experience with them. There are other groups for that. Movie Set Memes is not your personal army for justice—Witch-hunts are strictly forbidden. 6. Film Students are welcome! However don't say anything you may regret. Remember that your peers and professionals are on here and anything you say here CAN ACTUALLY affect your career. 7. TMZ type posts like actor drama or posts about upcoming blockbusters won’t be approved—Golden rule is if you post it, will someone who doesn’t work in the industry understand it? If the answer is “yes,” then it probably shouldn’t be posted... 8. Misusin' a meme? That’s a paddlin’... Your post doesn't have to be a meme, per se, however if you decide to use a popular image macro like Kermit drinking tea--please use it appropriately. If you're unsure, visit www.knowyourmeme.com . We welcome all forms of humor relating to the film production industry including meta jokes. 9. Don't waste the admins' time asking if "it's ok” to post something. Just post it and if it doesn't get approved, then it probably was too irrelevant or breaking some of these rules. Don't block admin. 10. Re-posts are allowed if they are presently relevant. It’s ok to post someone else’s meme or share a post from another group so long as you're not purposely promoting another group or page for your own personal gain. 11. Do not block admins. They are very sensitive. Have Fun! 
                </div>

                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 ~~SAD PUPPERS 420 PRESENTS~~ ~a nice place 2 find humor in ur sadness~ - -this is a space for compassionate humor, relatable memes, and sharing experiences. while it largely revolves around our experiences with depression and mental illness, the mods believe that its main purpose is to lighten the load. posts that are too heavy or lacking required content warnings may not be approved --please add CWs (content warnings) as requested. please treat subjects like suicide, rape, trauma, etc. with special care and TW or CW accordingly. Do not mock content warnings or else you will be banned. --we want to avoid this group being an echo chamber of negative feelings about ourselves and our relationships, so it is important that there is an aspect of humor in the post if it is a personal account / OC. please respect collective emotional boundaries. --while we encourage people to relate about difficult experiences here, this is not and cannot be a support group. it is too large for vulnerable discussions on traumatic subjects. posts/comments like these may be deleted. the mods cannot guarantee the safety of the space, but work to make it as safe as we can. SOME POSTING STANDARDS --if you think your post would need a trigger warning, reconsider if this is the right place to post it. --triggered jokes or joke content warnings are bannable --do not attempt spicy discourse or concern trolling on trigger warnings and their effectiveness --we consider the phrase "crippling depression" to be ableist and discourage its use in original content &amp; shared memes BAD / DISCOURAGED POSTS --journal-type oversharing of trauma or mundane events --related to the DSM, diagnosis or self-diagnosis --posts seeking help / in crisis --humorless self hatred --“guess i’ll die now” memes (often) --tag yourself and starter pack memes --tinder screenshots (with few exceptions) --anything featuring blood / gore --cutting references and imagery --overt suicide references --edgy posts or discourse about medication --general spicy discourse and hot takes (in posts &amp; comments) --political memes and academic discourse --anything shared from Buzzfeed and affiliates (Adam Ellis, etc) - IF YOU ARE IN AN UNSAFE OR EMERGENCY SITUATION (IN THE UNITED STATES), PLEASE CALL THE NATIONAL SUICIDE HOTLINE AT 1-800-273-8255!!! IF YOU CANNOT CALL A PREVENTION LIFELINE OR ARE IN ANOTHER COUNTRY AND FEEL THAT YOU MAY BE A THREAT TO YOURSELF, HERE ARE INTERNATIONAL RESOURCES: - http://www.iasp.info/resources/Crisis_Centres/ - http://www.suicide.org/international-suicide-hotlines.html - http://www.crisischat.org - https://www.imalive.org/ - http://www.7cups.com - http://nightline.ac.uk - http://www.samaritans.org &lt;3 for the love of puppers &lt;3 sad pupper non-militarized funtime facilitation crew

                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 The Punitentiary
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Punishing puns that get sent to the punitentiary. To keep things pun for everyone, we have a few rules: 1. No bigotry. Racism, sexism, transphobia, ableism, etc are not funny and aren't allowed here. 2. Sensitive subjects (suicide, abuse, violence, etc) don't belong here either. There's other places on the internet for dark humor. We want this place to be light. 3. Let's keep this group somewhat family-friendly, or at least PG. No lewd, NSFW, toilet-humor jokes. 4. For the love of everything sacred, no political jokes or religious jokes. 5. To make sure everyone's pun gets a chance at being enjoyed, limit your posting to about 3-4 puns a day. 6. The above rules do not cover every situation. The staff use their best judgement on how to handle things, but we are human. If you have questions/concerns, send one of us a PM. (Staff members are listed below.) Please note that we try to curtail repetition, so if your submissions doesn't make it through, it may have just been one that's been shared recently enough we don't want to have it in again for a time. Pun Staff: Pungeon Master (Admin): Karl Froelich (-Message him if questions/concerns), Sarah Bailey Punny Minions (Mods): Katherine Sweets, Scott Connelly, David Mattice-Mottle, Timothy Brockway, Andrew Richbell, Angèle Serré, Gay Bergman

                 LA Underground Comedy Network
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Welcome to the LA Underground Comedy Network! The Underground is meant to be an inside news source for great upcoming shows of all of the Amazingly talented performers around town! It's hard to stay up to date with what shows everyone is up to around to, so consider this a newsfeed to help you stay connected with news on shows, Newly released Sketches, and other funny news about performers and up and comers at the theater! Feel free to post any show's you're looking to promote, or any web content that you're trying to get some exposure on. Like Improv this community runs on support. This page will not conduct any transactions, but is merely a means for all of the regular fans of the theater to get in touch with each other and help out fellow Citizens to get to a show that might be sold out. Feel free to post if you're either Looking for tickets or Looking to get rid of tickets. Any agreements can be made via message over Facebook or through commenting, but PLEASE ABIDE BY THE THEATERS GUIDELINES to ensure that things run smoothly, and that everyone can stay happy. Just an FYI, I'm in no way responsible for the actions of the people on here. That being said, Please treat each other with respect and friendship since we're all fans and members of the Church of Comedy. Also just to reiterate, this an UNOFFICIAL group and is not associated with this group or theater, it is only a page for fans to interact and as a means of connecting with the community as a whole. I hope this helps all the other Addicts out there like me. This group is driven by Invites, so if you know someone who's interested Make sure to invite them!

                </div>

                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Jewish Humor
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 "With so many negative events taking place around the planet, sometimes it is refreshing to stand back for a moment and enjoy a good laugh! The Bible says : "A merry heart doeth good like a medicine, but a broken spirit drieth the bones.." In our present troubled world, watching &amp; listening to some Jewish humor is just what the Jewish doctor ordered! We can't just sit there in misery &amp; negativity. Even in the concentration camps, Jews were humorous. Research has revealed that the Jews in concentration camps created plays, told jokes because the only thing they could do was laugh at their own predicament, sad as it was, because there was no other escape &amp; the only other alternative was to go crazy altogether! Feeling different, feeling alienated, feeling persecuted, feeling that the only way you can deal with the world is to laugh because if you don't laugh you're going to cry and never stop crying -- that's probably what's responsible for the Jews having developed such a great sense of humor. The people who had the greatest reason to weep, learned more than anyone else how to laugh. I welcome you &amp; all Jews with open arms! I'll do my best to keep everyone well entertained. Let this group be like sunshine and be a joy &amp; a blessing in everyone's life! " 
                </div>

Rules: -Only puns are allowed as posts. *(Either in the picture or the heading.) -A post that isn't a pun will be deleted. *(This includes posts requesting puns.) -I reiterate, if it IS NOT A PUN, it will be DELETED. -Please keep posts light-hearted. *(Nothing too dark, nor blatantly offensive.) -Please be respectful to your fellow members. Drama/arguing in comments is strictly prohibited. This is a FRIENDLY atmosphere. If it cannot be settled reasonably, the comment thread will be removed. -Do not post puns making jokes about people dying. *(This includes celebrities and tragic events, but excludes fictional ones.) -Recent repeat posts will also be deleted. -Spam messages are grounds for instant banning. -No posts about religions of any kind. If you see anyone posting ads or other such nonsense, please notify a mod and we will promptly destroy them with extreme prejudice. -If you see a post that violates one of these rules, please tag a moderator or admin. We may not spot it. -Repeated breaking of rules will result in.... PUNishment. (No really. You'll be kicked out. Hence the "GTFO") -Have fun.

                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 I feel personally attacked by this relatable map
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 a group for Geography Memes and other Relatable Geospatial Content an overview of group guidelines: 1. NO EDGELORD BULLSHIT!!! We do not tolerate racism, sexism, homophobia, transmisogyny, or any other -isms. Be good to each other. Also, don't post content with any sort of racial or defamatory slurs in it, even if said slurs are used ironically. Doing any of this will result in a swift delete+permaban. 2. In a similar vein, don't post maps relating to ""edgy"" topics with the intention of baiting people (such as maps of average IQ scores by country). They always end badly. 3. Keep it GEOSPATIAL. This means content related to maps, geography, cartography, and GIS, but can also extend to allied fields like urban planning, transportation, earth science, etc. Any completely unrelated content will be promptly deleted. 4. "Stereotype maps" of particular regions will be promptly deleted. They're usually offensive and almost always lazy. 5. Most map-related content doesn't require trigger warnings or content warnings, but if your post features a common trigger (i.e. sex, violence, suicide, etc.) please add a tw/cw to your post, and if any group member (esp an admin) asks you to put one on your post, please do so without making a fuss. Any tw/cw jokes will be deleted. 6. In the spirit of fostering good map literacy, if your post contains a map based on actual data (ie it's not a joke or a shitpost), please include a link to the source where you found it! 7. Don't advertise your own facebook page or group unless you clear it with us first. any spam posts or random advertisements will be deleted. 8. To avoid reposts, scroll down the group for a few posts before sharing a link. we may delete your post if someone else has posted it recently. 9. If someone mentions the word 'Israel' or 'Palestine' in passing, and you start an argument, we will ban you. Do not ask "Do you mean _________?" 10. Any posts that explicitly violate the guidelines above will be deleted without warning. 11. If you see a questionable post, please smash that mf "Report to Admin" button. For problematic comments sections, tag any of us in said comment thread. Also, if you've been banned from the group for whatever reason, for the love of god, don't send abusive messages to any of the admins (this has actually happened before and it is extremely Not Cool). 12. Above all, please just be good to each other. We want this group to be a fun and enjoyable space for everyone, and reserve the right to remove any people or content which detracts from this goal. full post here: https://www.facebook.com/groups/dankgeographymemes/permalink/1747868118587411/
                </div>

                 POST SCREENSHOTS OF LEABS. 98.6% or more of the content should be that. Go post tired memes elsewhere. Go do IDPOL (identity politics) elsewhere. Funny, overly-dramatic leabs = fun. If you post a leab of yourself leabing this gronp, whether for real or “ironically,” you will be blocked. And you won’t get to see whether we deleted your post or just deleted you. No meta-leabs. It’s been done; we voted on it, we don’t want it anymore. 4) Language policing won't be happening unless it's outright rude as fuck and directed at a specific individual. So please don't try and make this into Leftbook. 5) No members get to block any Admins. We can still see you and know you've done it. 6.) Do NOT report posts or comments. You will be blocked. Tag a couple of Abmins or just ask for help if you can’t do that. 7.) It’s going to be tempting, but NO POLITICAL DISCOURSE. This includes IDPOL (identify politics). Don’t be an asshat. Period.                 </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Welcome to Simpsons Bortposting! -TL;DR for lurkers &amp; commenters: enjoy the OC and keep dickish comments to yourself. If you’re going to post content, read on: This group is all about creating new memes and shit, enjoying other people’s creations, and sharing them to spread the love. We’re all about creating a steady flow of new OC, which brings us to what is pretty much the main rule: ***Only post shit you made yourself.*** Some people like to watermark their content with the group logo in the group’s files but that’s totally optional. All we care about is that you post your own OC. ================================== If an admin deletes your OC thinking it’s a repost, message us and let us know. ================================== Read the group rules in the “about” section for a better idea of what we do here. But at the end of the day, we just want everyone to have a good time. That’s about it, go nuts borterinos!

                 Hello, Guys and Gals Although the group is called ‘Mechanic Memes Only,’ there is so much content submitted that we do sometimes allow things that are not necessarily a “meme.” These non-meme posts can include pics, videos, gifs, cartoons, drawings, etc., but please remember that context and content is important. Although our members come from all around the world, this group is mostly English speaking. If you post something that has been translated from another language, please confirm that it makes sense before submitting it. ALL POSTS/COMMENTS MUST BE IN ENGLISH.                 <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 A Group Where You Can Only Say Yikes
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 😬 YIKES 😬 This is literally a group where you can only say yikes. This is a left-leaning, lighthearted, SFW group. Allowed: -“Yikes”, “Yike”, “Sekiy” -Tagging members/mods -Symbols, Emojis, Emoticons, Numbers -Pictures, Gifs, Videos -Memes! Especially Yikes memes. (Yes, that means you can screenshot text and post. If y’all abuse this, we will have to reconsider so use sparingly.) Not allowed: -Literally any word that is not “Yikes” or approved variants. -“Yi(you’re not clever if you do this)kes” -“ekiY” -”Yikes” in other languages. -Tagging groups -Links in the comments -Captions on posts that aren’t approved variants. No sentences, just pure yikes. -Spelling words with emoji. There’s a fine line between emojis and non-yikes. Don’t cross it. -Watch parties. You will be banned. -Anything that requires a CW/TW. This includes: Anything you couldn’t show a stereotypical boss or grandmother. Racism, Transphobia, homophobia, misogyny, slut shaming, pedophilia, incest, animal abuse, child abuse, sexual violence, nudity, porn, etc. EVEN IF YOU’RE SAYING YIKES TO IT. We don’t wanna see it and you’ll be banned. Bad times for everyone. —Yikes ≠ Cringe: Just because something is edgy or gross does not mean it belongs here. Post submissions are pre-screened by moderators. If we do not like your content, we may ban you. (Helpful hint: Look at the kinds of posts that are accepted first, and get a feel for what is good content before you submit something) —If you post something other than yikes on accident, quickly edit it to say yikes or you will be banned. Saying “Edit: yikes” in your edited comment will also get you banned. We just want yikes, that’s it. —If someone is making non-yikes comments, harassing you, or creating unwanted discourse, we encourage tagging mods or reporting the comments to an admin. Snitches get praise! —If you feel you or someone else was unjustly banned, take it up in @Discourse Regarding A “Group Where You Can Only Say Yikes”. You may also apply for representation at @The Law Offices of Yikes, Sekiy, &amp; Yike, Esq. Please do NOT message mods or admins about bans. —Do not argue in this group. Take it to the discourse group. Too much discourse (even with gifs or photos) in this group will result in muting/a ban. 🏳️‍🌈🏳️‍🌈🏳️‍🌈🏳️‍🌈🏳️‍🌈🏳️‍🌈🏳️‍🌈 We have Yikes Shirts! Available on etsy at tinyurl.com/onlyyikes - proceeds go to an LGBT non-profit run by the admin.

               <div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 VET Tv - Veteran Television
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 ATTENTION! The VET Tv Facebook group was created for those who love dark military humor. If you want to reminisce about the good ole times on deployment, try to reconnect with some rack mates, or just love reading and relating to other people’s stories… this place is for you. This is about community, so keep the negativity out. Mission: To recreate and parody the military experience to make people feel good. Vision: To bring the entire military community together through laughter. Ground Rules to ensure we aren’t just like every other Facebook Group: 1. I know we advocate for Rated R content on VET Tv but since this is still on Facebook, let’s follow their guidelines. 2. Keep the bullshit out. We're here to have fun and enjoy each other's stories, not to be dickheads or do anything that doesn't serve the mission." 3. Nothing overtly sexual, racist or distasteful. 4. Limit the reposts. Lots of funny stuff in the world but we want your voice. We want to know who you are, hear your stories and thoughts, and see your pictures and videos about life in the military. 5. Advertising or Fundraising posts must be approved by VET Tv. Please email us if you have any inquiries. 6. We are not a buy/sell/trade group. We’ll leave that to Craigslist. Examples of the kind of posts we prefer: Why did you get out? Why did you join? Let’s see those boot camp pictures! What issues are active-duty soldiers really pissed about? What’s your favorite military phrase? What’s your favorite thing to do in your off time? Any funny boot camp stories? What’s the craziest place you had sex during work hours? What do you wish you could change about the military? Much Love, The VET Tv Crew ***Disclaimer*** By participating in this group, you understand and agree that any storylines, character descriptions or other creative ideas which you may express become the property of the writers and producers completely and without any claim from you whatsoever (this just means if we like your stories and use them in a show, you can’t sue us). You further agree that you will not post copyrighted material or material owned or claimed by any third party without specifically and expressly stating such facts. Contact: info@veterantv.com
                </div>

                 Law School Memes for Edgy T14s
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Law Memes for 3Ls, 2Ls, and those filthy 1Ls. ---------------------------------------------------- The Model Rules of LSMFET14s Professional Responsibility: (i) Definition(s): Meme: What is a meme? who the hell knows. We’re flexible on what a meme is or is not: Generally, we will keep a nonmemey post IF (a) the post is funny and law related then that’s ok or (b) if the post isn’t funny but it leads to hilarious comments or it spawns meta memes, then we are likely keeping it up. Edgy: Dank memes. (1) Don't be unreasonably assholish. It’s an internet meme group; snark comes with the territory. Just don’t be unreasonable about it. What’s unreasonable? ¯\_(ツ)_/¯ figure it out. (2) Be culturally / socially aware. This means not making racist/sexist/ableist/etc memes/comments. Please report any offensive memes/comments. (a) Know your context and know your audience. This is the age of BLM and #MeToo. Sometimes even seemingly benign jokes can reinforce harmful stereotypes or attitudes / prejudices / actions, or they can be particularly hurtful in a given time period. For example, posting This Is America memes that make light of killing black people (even if this is not the explicit goal of the joke) or posting 2nd Amendment jokes after a mass shooting might not go over well. (b) Punch up, not down. In addition to being generally aware of your context, try to punch up (eg do make fun of Harvard for being elitist, don’t make fun of a school for being lower ranked). Not everyone in this group is in a T14 school, and being in a T14 doesn't mean shit. This group’s name is meant to be funny, not exclusive. All law students are welcome here (but Texas is on thin ice). All people are welcome here. (3) Admins and mods reserve the right to delete a post or ban anyone for any reason. (4) We r here 2 promote gay space communism. (5) Toilet humor is strictly prohibited unless it’s from Sadie Hillier (6) Be excellent to each other (7) Reposts from other pages/groups and posts with hyperlinks will generally not be accepted. Why? Because they tend to be low effort. Screenshot the article or post if you really want to share it. Notes of Meme Committee on Rules— 1 - 2 Note to Subdivision (b) This clause does not include jellyfish people. Even tho we said all people are welcome here that does not include jellyfish people. We do not want the medusozoa agenda on this meme page. ---------------------------------------------------- Fabulous Law Memes for Unsuppressible Fruity Queens [https://www.facebook.com/groups/296927407803417/ ] is an offshoot meme group of LSMFET14S, and any law student/lawyer who identifies as LGBTQ is welcome! ---------------------------------------------------- Law School Housing Bank: https://docs.google.com/spreadsheets/d/1BCNHKt0C2Lr0UB4Ff1JReesoFnfkUVSBUnc0_PHCA9g/edit#gid=1808274498

               <div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Military Humor And More
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Group formed 2013 by Steven Eppley updated-12-5-19 ***Please read all of the rules before asking to join.*** This is a Private group, only members can see posts. This group practices and will adhere to OPSEC. Operational Security is keeping quiet about what you're doing, when, where, and how. ** For the security of our group- We now require all prospective members to verify that they are either a Veteran or Dependents of a Veteran.You will be required to answer the membership question in order to be accepted into this group. Thank you This is a family-oriented group, therefore no profanity or vulgarity is permitted. A violation of the rules will result in you being banned from the group. As a member of this group you are responsible for reading and abiding by all of the rules. ***Abbreviations or acronyms of any profanity word is not permitted *** General forum rules : 1. Be polite and respect the other members. We have members from many countries and different cultures here so please be aware of this as well when posting! We also have women, children &amp; grandchildren who have access to this group as we are a family group! Respect them as you would like to be respected. 2. The following are not accepted in posts, but not limited to; Flaming, Baiting, Name Calling, Country Bashing, Spamming, Hate, political, Religion-bashing or anti-religious comments, Religious proselytizing, sexual, racist, anti-military, graphic, obscene photos and language;transgender, gay or LGBT jokes, or if it is just plain disgusting. Not only will the post be removed, the person posting may also be removed. 3. Threatening an Admin with the use of profanity will also result in being immediately banned. 4. No controversial post shall be posted . In other words, submitting a post that will cause members to ramble on &amp; on about pro's and con's of a person, group, or content will not be put on the board. 5. Behavior that will also lead to an immediate ban includes: -Posting anything regarding a terrorist organization 6. Since our admins cannot screen comments on shared items, members of our group are responsible for the content of pictures and comments made on share discussions on other pages or groups. If there are excessive posts in the other page/group, Admins may delete posts at their own discretion. For the best outcome, members of this group should download pictures to their device and reload them clean to our group and, if needed, copy &amp; paste any text - cleaning up any unacceptable language. 7. Asking for monetary support for various causes including GoFundMe links is not allowed in this group. Asking for funds for any reasons or causes is absolutely forbidden.*Any advertising for any commercial sites is not allowed. 8. Violating Facebook's Community Standards will result in removal,banned and blocked from the group,including pending posts.                  FB Comedy Writing Group
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Open to all comics/comedy writers/ aspiring humorists. In order to maintain the quality of the group, we have found it necessary to impose the following rules: To join: 1. You must have friends in the group, OR 2. You look like a comedian in your profile, OR 3. Describe your intent as part of your membership request. Admins will review all applications. Once in: Feel free to post thoughts, premises, stories, or any ideas for feedback. From developed bits to random thoughts, let's all get better together. Keep it related to WRITING comedy, posts about comedy are fine if they don't get too out of control, but DO NOT post for promotional purposes only DO NOT promote shows DO NOT post unoriginal content unless your purpose is to critique / inform. DO NOT make RACIST or SEXIST posts. In an interest to maintain a productive environment, anyone posting anything RACIST or SEXIST will have their post deleted and will be removed from the group. RACIAL and SEXUAL humor are ok, just nothing overtly hateful. Yes this is subjective and if you aren't sure, it might be best for you to try your joke elsewhere. On this rule, there are no questions, no exceptions, and no contingencies. If you cannot abide by those rules, perhaps this is not the group for you.

              <div class="_8tn0">
               <div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Ozzy Man's Video Submission Zone
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 An extra place to send me videos that ya reckon would be good for commentary and critical analysis. If you've shot something original yourself, you can also send a copy to submit@ozzyman.com RULES: 1) Limited picture/meme posts will be approved. I'm mostly keen on looking at videos when I have the bloody time. 2) Absolutely add likes and comments to videos you agree would be good with some cheeky commentary. Extra opinions are welcome and a good indicator that I need to listen up. 3) Please don't link to anything too graphic or overly sexualised (people getting injured is cool, let's avoid death though, that's kinda where the line is at when I'm lookin' at stuff). 4) If a video is not necessarily commentary-worthy, but you reckon it's funny as fuck and you think other Ozzy Man fans would also find it funny, you can still share it and it will have a fair chance of getting approved. 5) Blocking admin or mods to evade 'em will result in your removal from the group. MISC: I am blunt. I am vulgar. But I am not a bully. Most name-calling that occurs in an Ozzy Man commentary is between wildlife when I give them characterisation. Think twice before submitting a video where you believe the core goal should be to roast, shame, or gang-up on someone. I do believe any topic is capable of being satirised (politics, religion, gender/relationships), but execution is key. If too much content that's submitted is loaded with an agenda then it won't be approved. Different people find different things funny, that's the great thing about comedy, but yeah nah yeah, too much of an agenda can kill the fun (this is something I myself have learnt at times as the audience has broadened). Overall, posting is enabled again, but I am keeping the Post Approval option on for a while longer. Apologies if it's a bit slow to get things approved at the moment. If a few people are keen to moderate then send us an email to ozzymanreviews@gmail.com The goal of this group was just to have an extra video submissions zone outside of the private inboxes, so I could see trends a little easier when multiple people are requesting something. Maybe it'll be okay, or maybe it will end up needing too much maintenance and the one on one submission process in the inbox is still the best way to go. Dunno. Open to the experiment is all. Cheers!

                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 what does it mean
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 What Does It Mean is an educational community for explaining and asking absolutely anything, from absurd memes to abstract concepts. Members are encouraged to take all questions seriously, and answer with the utmost sincerity and consideration. (Mostly just another tag group) • Pending members MUST answer all three questions to be considered for approval. • All members MUST read, accept and adhere to the following group rules: https://www.facebook.com/groups/890289887772434/about/ • Please also read this list of memes we do not tolerate: https://www.facebook.com/groups/890289887772434/permalink/1413755218759229/ (Check the group announcements tab if this link isn't working!) • If you see any problematic or rule-breaking behaviour, feel free to tag any of the following admins/moderators: https://www.facebook.com/groups/890289887772434/admins/ Alternatively, if no admins/moderators are available, you can use the "report to group admins" feature, but please do not "report to Facebook". Please bear in mind that mods are not paid to moderate; we may not always be available. We try our hardest to respond to all tags/reports. • Top 5 reasons your post was not approved: 1) It's a re-post, posted too soon after the original. 2) Graphic/upsetting content without a CW (we may post on your behalf). 3) Blatantly ironic use of a CW (get a new joke). 4) Attachment unavailable/broken link. 5) A 'Loss' meme (check the banned memes post for the reasons why). Be kind to each other and happy learning!

And I can't believe I have to type this in the rules. Have some common sense. --- Do not post memes with racist, sexist, misogynistic, transphobic, ableist, etc content, eg: derogatory names that demean women, mocking people with disabilities or mental illness, for example, etc :) **** Use trigger/content warnings on posts that need them, and nest in comments. Also just consider not posting triggering content in here ¯\_(ツ)_/¯ Put any NSFW content in the comments, not in your initial post as a courtesy to others. Posts that are reported with NSFW content not posted in the comments are subject to deletion. Members also subject to removal from the group. NSFW content can be text and/or images. Err on the side of caution and just put the meme in the comments. Again, NSFW content includes that of sexual content. There are also children in the group. Admins have specified that all NSFW content be posted in the comments and not the original post. Any post not adhering to this can be deleted without notice. But we will take screenshots. **** Tell your friends to read this when you add them. BE COOL :) --- And if you see something please just hit report to admin :) Reporting to the admin doesn't mean anyone is in trouble...we're not your parents. We'll just delete the pic.                  UCR Dank Memes for Quarantined Tweens
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Official Constitution of UCR Dank Memes for Rejected Tweens Or Whatever 1) No personal attacks, harassment, racism, sexism, etc I mean honestly, does this need elaboration? Don’t be a dick. 2) No doxxing Posting other people’s personal information in an attempt to out them in some way is not okay. Any member that posts information which has a reasonable expectation of privacy will be banned immediately. 3) Any UCR or college-related memes are acceptable but original memes are highly encouraged We want this page to be primarily high quality original content. Memes that are unrelated to college are allowed, but only in moderation (ways to control this will be discussed). This will not become a meme dump for people that browse Reddit and iFunny and want attention. Anything that is not a meme and irrelevant to the page will be deleted. 4) No political proselytizing We are here to post memes, not push our political views on others. You can post memes that involve politicians as punchlines as long as it isn’t explicitly or implicitly pushing a political view. Ex: Trump flipping through infrastructure binder “Me studying for finals”; Hillary overreacting to fireworks “Me taking ecstasy at Spring Splash for the first time” *these aren’t the best but you get the point 5) Don’t start drama It’s pretty obvious when people are deliberately trying to start drama in a comment section. Whether or not you are is for the mods to determine. 6) The mods reserve the right to create new rules as they see fit New rules can be amended to this constitution and applied retroactively at the discretion of the mods. 7) Most importantly, don’t take things too seriously Amendments af: 8/29/17 1) New schedule: During the week, posts are restricted to college-related and meta-related memes. On weekends, any subjects are fine 2) Drama is okay as long as it’s funny and doesn’t get too out of hand. 3/21/18 3) Disregard Amendment 1. ONLY UCR or College related memes are allowed. OC is HIGHLY encouraged. Mods may or may not delete memes that are not OC or memes that were shared from another meme page 6/10/18 4) In addition to Amendment 3, mods may or may not inform you about a post that was deleted. Please reach out to a mod to find out why your post was deleted. 5) In order to avoid content saturation on the meme page by one user, please limit your posts to 1 meme every 5 hours or 1 meme every 5 posts. (e.g. wait for at least 5 memes to be posted before you post another meme or wait for 5 hours before you post again). 6) Smurf accounts are allowed… for now. For a completely updated constitution, visit https://docs.google.com/document/d/1OCK1WwcQei0k-6vWggRd0QmqSQGfrVyIl-uq9BCwl8g/edit

                 So Cal Comedian Connection
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 The purpose of this group is to join all comedians who do/will perform in the Southern California area. Utilize this group to connect with other comedians regarding shows, gig opportunities, charity events, last minute openings and where ever else you can see a need to connect with other comics. Share any concerns and issues that you would like to receive input/feedback from other comedians as well. You may also use this group page to share any resources that you have found to help you in your comic careers. **this page is not for constant event promotions- that's what your wall is for**

                 MemeAndComedy
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Meme is life. Comedy is, too. Cash App $Aquaman34 $15 to be mod Group Rules and Expectations: Above anything else, "MemeAndComedy" values free speech and the exercise thereof. With that being said, we do have a few rules. The rules listed below are by no means exhaustive. The Admins and Moderators reserve the right, at their discretion, to delete posts, remove and permanently block members, in order to maintain group focus. 1. Whatever you upload must be a meme or something comedic. This does not necessarily mean that the memes you upload have to be funny. 2. Racism in any form is not tolerated. If you upload a meme or post anything found to be racially insensitive, your post will be deleted and you may be banned permanently from the group. 3. It is best to post at least once or twice per hour. Members who are found to be crowding the group's timeline may have posts removed and kicked out the group (although this need not be a permanent ban). 4. The best practice is to save memes to your phone or computer and upload them to "MemeAndComedy.com" directly. We highly discourage sharing memes from other groups or pages. 5. Whenever possible, try to use the hashtag #memeandcomedy when uploading posts. This will help the group grow faster ( which is currently 1k new members every 24 hours). 6. Please, although this is not a requirement, keep sexually related posts to a minimum. This is not a sex group and certain posts can land you in Facebook jail. Be a little more creative and post memes that are thought provoking and funny. 7. Share something from this group at least once a day. At least, lol 8. Respect each other. Abusive members will be removed from the group. Our Moderators are good at what they do and you never know when one is looking, lol. 9. Your Admins are Antavius Flagg and Antonio Flagg ( group Creator). Search them and follow. 10. DO NOT ADVERTISE OTHER GROUPS! This will get you banned permanently. The only group or websites that should be promoted here are those associated with http://www.memeandcomedy.com 11. Finally, have fun and remember that everything here is in good humor!

Look for the link in the Recommended by the Admins section of this group. *If you have a great pic that could be turned into a meme, share it.* I'm going to keep the rules short, sweet and simple, but they are rules that we all must adhere to. No Blocking of admin/mods at any time. No personal attacks on group members. As soon as you address another member with terms like "you, you're, your" or tagging someone in a disagreement YOU will be banned from this group! NO HOMOPHOBIC OR RACIST COMMENTS/POSTS/MEMES WILL BE TOLERATED! No advertisement of any kind, except by group admins. No Porn Videos. Failure to adhere to any of our rules will get you deleted and banned from the group. Keep this group LIGHT and FUN! Exchange Memes and get to know your fellow group members. Please contact an Admin/Mod if you see anyone breaching the group rules. Thanks!

              <div class="_8uly">
               <div class="_8wo2"></div>
              </div>
              <div class="_8tn0">
               <div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Intelectuales Con Humor
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Hola, intelectuales, este grupo está realizado especialmente para ustedes. Les invitamos a leer lo siguiente: ---- CONCEPTO DEL GRUPO: Este grupo se compone de dos premisas y lo dice su nombre "intelectuales y con humor"; no todas las publicaciones tienen que ser con humor, pero sí todas deben tener cierto grado de intelectualidad. Definamos intelectual: Que realiza actividades donde predomina el uso de la inteligencia. Esto no significa que se deban hacer solo publicaciones de ciencias, lectura o filosofía, sino a que las publicaciones no deben ser para nada básicas, deben construir el intelecto, valores, ser interesantes, curiosas y hasta fantásticas. Nada de humor simplón, piolines con reflexiones o publicaciones donde se burlen de la desgracias ajenas. Pensemos en este grupo como un grupo exclusivo, donde tu forma de pensar y valores son tu pase VIP. Si quieres saber un poco más de esto, de lo que piensan los miembros y tal vez comentar qué te parece, te invito a ir a esta publicación: https://www.facebook.com/groups/intelectualesconhumor/permalink/369896506890569/ ---- ¿QUÉ PUBLICAR Y QUÉ NO? Si ya eres miembro y tienes dudas en cuanto a qué publicar o te preguntas por qué no te aprobaron una publicación, puedes leer esta publicación que lo explica a detalle: https://www.facebook.com/groups/intelectualesconhumor/permalink/459455737934645/ Si leyendo eso, aún crees que tu publicación debió ser aprobada, En el siguiente vínculo puedes comentar tu publicación y pedir el detalle del porqué no se te aprobó (no sin antes ver los comentarios de otros miembros, ahí puede estar tu respuesta). https://www.facebook.com/groups/intelectualesconhumor/permalink/459276004619285/ ---- PREGUNTAS FRECUENTES: Aquí puedes encontrar respuestas a preguntas frecuentes que se hacen en el grupo: https://www.facebook.com/groups/intelectualesconhumor/permalink/459460751267477/ ---- NORMAS DEL GRUPO: Se encuentran secciones más abajo (si es que estás en la pestaña de información). ---- Los invitamos a hacer grande este grupo, compartamos e invitemos, que de los grupos de contenido cochambre, ya hay muchos. ¡A disfrutar!
                </div>
               </div>

              <div class="_8tn0">
               <div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 MEMES DEL DIA...
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Hola, bienvenidos al grupo es gratis. Los memes son eventos chistosos de acuerdo a una accion cotidiana, politica, trabajo o deportes... puedes subir fotos chuscas que den risa, dar like si te gusta, compartir a tus amigos. Eviten subir pornografia o fotos de desnudo que ofendan, memes politicos o religiosos que ofendan a otros miembros. El administrador de este grupo se da el derecho de aceptar o no miembros, publicaciones y comentarios negativos, borrara y dara de baja a miembros problematicos, o quienes suban publicidad personal o comercial. Este grupo esta hecho para divertirse, si algun miembro busca lo contrario sera mejor que busque otros grupos de su conveniencia. Gracia de nuevo y bienvenidos a la diversiony con posiblilidades grandes de hacer amigos.
                </div>
